Urgent Care wait times from publicly available sources, and to present them in a single location for public benefit.\n    Find current ER wait times near you, and see how they compare to recent trends around the United States.\n    Historical data can be downloaded using our API.\n    The data shown here is updated every 15 minutes.\n    Facilities without live updating wait times do not appear on
